$(document).ready(function() {
    "use strict";

    if($('.glb-grid-24')){

        var cardId = '#ge-card-classificacao-4511b537-e979-4358-a3ce-9ab19ea19b1b',
                classificacaoFeedReady = false,
                classificacaoCardReady = false;

            $(document).on('bastian-feed-card_rendered', cardId, function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Feed Ready');
                classificacaoFeedReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

            $(document).on('card-classificacao-ready', function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Card Ready');
                classificacaoCardReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

        var initCardClassificacao = function(){
            if(classificacaoCardReady && classificacaoFeedReady){
                $('#ge-card-classificacao-4511b537-e979-4358-a3ce-9ab19ea19b1b').show();
            }
        }
    }

    try {

      var classificacao = new CardClassificacao({
        context: '#ge-card-classificacao-4511b537-e979-4358-a3ce-9ab19ea19b1b'
      });

      var classificacaoTracking = new CardClassificacaoTracking("4511b537-e979-4358-a3ce-9ab19ea19b1b");

    } catch (err) {}

});

                        Taça Libertadores

        </ul>

$(document).ready(function() {
    "use strict";

    if($('.glb-grid-24')){

        var cardId = '#ge-card-classificacao-d01387cf-12cf-480e-bad5-74a5d151b28f',
                classificacaoFeedReady = false,
                classificacaoCardReady = false;

            $(document).on('bastian-feed-card_rendered', cardId, function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Feed Ready');
                classificacaoFeedReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

            $(document).on('card-classificacao-ready', function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Card Ready');
                classificacaoCardReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

        var initCardClassificacao = function(){
            if(classificacaoCardReady && classificacaoFeedReady){
                $('#ge-card-classificacao-d01387cf-12cf-480e-bad5-74a5d151b28f').show();
            }
        }
    }

    try {

      var classificacao = new CardClassificacao({
        context: '#ge-card-classificacao-d01387cf-12cf-480e-bad5-74a5d151b28f'
      });

      var classificacaoTracking = new CardClassificacaoTracking("d01387cf-12cf-480e-bad5-74a5d151b28f");

    } catch (err) {}

});
